### libgphoto2 Internal Commands

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ricoh/g3.txt

Overview of internal commands for camera control and data management.

```APIDOC
## Internal FTP Style Commands

### PRET

#### Description
Partial retrieve command. Likely used for retrieving specific parts of data.

### CCTL

#### Description
Control command. Its exact function is not fully specified but is likely for camera control operations.

### SINF

#### Description
Command to set information. Its specific use case is not detailed.

### FMT

#### Description
Format card command. Used to format the camera's storage card.

### ATTR

#### Description
Command to get or set attributes. The specific attributes are not detailed.

### PWOF

#### Description
Power off command. Used to turn off the camera.

### SDIS <filename>

#### Description
Set distinction command. The meaning of 'distinction' is unclear.

### GDIS

#### Description
Get distinction command. Related to the SDIS command, retrieves distinction information.

### ABOR

#### Description
Abort command. Typically used to abort ongoing data transfers.

### FUPL

#### Description
Upload command. Used for uploading files to the camera.

### FDWL

#### Description
Command for file download list. Likely retrieves a list of files available for download.

### GFCI

#### Description
Get file count information. Retrieves the number of files in a directory.

### GFGI

#### Description
Get file group information. Possibly retrieves information about groups of files.

### SGID

#### Description
Set file group information. Used to set information related to file groups.

### VER

#### Description
Get version information.

#### Response Example
```
200 9.2 01.06
```

### FDAT folder/file

#### Description
Get file date command. Retrieves the modification date of a file or folder.

#### Response Example
```
200 date=2003:10:08 16:57:06
```
or
```
200 date=%s
```

### INFO folder/file

#### Description
Get information about a folder or file, including byte size, width, and height.

#### Response Example
```
200 %d byte W=%d H=%d K=%d
```

### GSID

#### Description
Get SD card ID. Retrieves the unique identifier for the SD card.

#### Response Example
```
200 SD ID=%02x%02x%02x%02x%02x%02x%02x%02x
```

### GCID

#### Description
Get camera ID. Retrieves the unique identifier for the camera.

#### Response Example
```
451 -GCID command failure
```
or
```
200 CameraID=%s
```

### TIME

#### Description
Get current time from the camera.

#### Response Example
```
200 %02d%02d/%02d/%02d %02d:%02d:%02d
```
or
```
200 2003/10/11 19:47:23
```

### NLST

#### Description
List files in a directory.

#### Response Example
```
150 data connection for -NLST.
  ... data blocks ...
250 -NLST command success.
```

### GTPN

#### Description
Get total photo number. Retrieves the total count of photos on the camera.

#### Response Example
```
200 TotalPhotoNo=%d
```

### RTST

#### Description
Get RTC status. Retrieves the status of the Real-Time Clock.

#### Response Example
```
200 RTC status=%d
```

### DCAP /EXT0

#### Description
Get capacity information for a storage device (e.g., /EXT0).

#### Response Example
```
200 /EXT0 capacity 63520768 byte,free 39043072 byte.
```

### SRET filename

#### Description
Seek Retrieve command. Downloads image data starting from a specific seek position. Used to retrieve thumbnails.

#### Response Example
```
150 %d byte Seek=%d W=%d H=%d S=%d for -SRET.
  ... bytes+seek image data ...
250 -SRET command success.
```

### STOR size filename

#### Description
Store command. Uploads a file of a specified size to the camera.

#### Response Example
```
150 ... 
  ... data transfer ... 
200 done
```

## Generic FTP Style Commands

### CWD folder

#### Description
Change working directory command.

#### Response Example
```
501 CWD command failure
```
or
```
250 CWD command success.
```

### RETR file

#### Description
Retrieve file command. Downloads a file from the camera.

#### Response Example
```
150 data connection for RETR.(%d)
  ... data , %d bytes ...
250 RETR command success.
```

### DELE file

#### Description
Delete file command. Removes a file from the camera.

#### Response Example
```
250 DELE command success.
```
or
```
500 DELE command failure
```

### RMD dir

#### Description
Remove directory command. Deletes a directory from the camera.

#### Response Example
```
250 RMD command success.
```
or
```
500 RMD command failure
```

### MKD dir

#### Description
Make directory command. Creates a new directory on the camera.

#### Response Example
```
257 "%s" directory created.
```
or
```
500 MKD command failure
```

### RNFR name

#### Description
Rename From command. Specifies the old name of a file or directory for renaming.

### RNTO name

#### Description
Rename To command. Specifies the new name for a file or directory during a rename operation.

```

### Image Settings Configuration

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/sony-dsc-rx0.txt

Endpoints for configuring image-related settings, such as image size and ISO sensitivity.

```APIDOC
## GET /main/imgsettings/imagesize

### Description
Retrieves or sets the desired image size (resolution) for captured photos.

### Method
GET/PUT

### Endpoint
/main/imgsettings/imagesize

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **value** (RADIO) - Required - The desired image size. Accepted values are '0' (Large), '1' (Medium), '2' (Small).

### Request Example (Set to Large)
```json
{
  "request": "PUT /main/imgsettings/imagesize?value=0"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **imagesize** (RADIO) - The current image size setting.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "imagesize": "Large"
}

## GET /main/imgsettings/iso

### Description
Retrieves or sets the ISO sensitivity (film speed) for image capture.

### Method
GET/PUT

### Endpoint
/main/imgsettings/iso

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **value** (RADIO) - Required - The desired ISO speed. Accepted values range from '0' (Auto ISO) to '39' (409600), with additional multi-frame noise reduction options.

### Request Example (Set to ISO 100)
```json
{
  "request": "PUT /main/imgsettings/iso?value=5"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **iso** (RADIO) - The current ISO speed setting.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "iso": "100"
}
```
```

### Device Properties Listing (Conceptual)

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/nikon-p2.txt

This conceptual example demonstrates how to retrieve and display the supported properties of a camera, including their IDs, names, and read/write capabilities. It assumes functions to access camera properties are available.

```c
#include <gphoto2.h>

int main() {
    GPContext *context = g_context_new();
    Camera *camera;
    int ret;

    ret = camera_new(context, &camera);
    if (ret != GP_OK) {
        fprintf(stderr, "Failed to initialize camera.\n");
        return 1;
    }

    CameraWidget *config;
    ret = gp_camera_get_config(camera, &config, context);
    if (ret == GP_OK) {
        printf("Device Properties Supported:\n");
        // Assuming navigation and retrieval of widgets representing properties
        // CameraWidget *root_widget = config;
        // CameraWidget *prop_widget;
        // ret = gp_camera_get_single_config(camera, "config_section_name", &prop_widget, context); // Example
        // if (ret == GP_OK) {
        //    const char *label;
        //    gp_widget_get_label(prop_widget, &label);
        //    printf("  %s\n", label);
        // }
        gp_widget_free(config);
    }

    camera_exit(camera, context);
    g_object_unref(context);

    return 0;
}
```

### Response

- **Current** (string) - The current white balance mode (e.g., "Automatic", "Daylight").
- **Choices** (array of objects) - Available white balance modes and their corresponding values.
  - **value** (integer) - The numerical value for the white balance mode.
  - **label** (string) - The descriptive label for the white balance mode.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "Current": "Automatic",
  "Choices": [
    {"value": 0, "label": "Automatic"},
    {"value": 1, "label": "Daylight"},
    // ... other choices
  ]
}
```
```

```APIDOC
## PUT /main/imgsettings/whitebalance

### Description
Sets the white balance setting.

### Method
PUT

### Endpoint
/main/imgsettings/whitebalance

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **Current** (integer) - The numerical value of the desired white balance mode.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "Current": 1
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **Success** (boolean) - Indicates if the operation was successful.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "Success": true
}
```
```

### Generate XML for PTP Command in C

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/olympus.txt

Illustrates the process of generating an XML structure for a PTP (Picture Transfer Protocol) command using the `generate_xml` function. This involves setting PTP parameters like Code, Nparam, and Param1 before generation.

```c
ptp.Code = 0x1016;
ptp.Nparam = 1;
ptp.Param1 = 0x5007;
generate_xml(&ptp, "abcd", 4);
return;
}
```

### Get Picture File Info 2 (libgphoto2)

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/sigma-fp.txt

Retrieves detailed information about a picture file. This command (0x902d) is sent with no arguments and receives a data payload containing file metadata. The response includes size and other file properties.

```c
/* Opcode: 0x902d */
/* Arguments: none */
/* Command: getpictfileinfo2 */
/* Response size: 0x38 bytes (example) */
/* Response snippet:
   0x902d: from cam: 0x38 bytes, with some info data
   4800000002002d9050000000
   38
   00 00 00 01
   00 00 00 0c
   00 00 00
   80 05 00 57
   c2 b8 07 00
   24000000...
*/
```

### libgphoto2 Command Reference (J-L)

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/barbie/Protocol.txt

Details the commands from 'J' to 'L' for the libgphoto2 protocol. Includes command data bytes, response data bytes, and a description of the command's function.

```text
CMD	CMD DATA BYTES		RESP DATA BYTES		Description
---	-----------------------	---------------------	-----------------------
J	2 (value: LSB, MSB)		2 (error, value)	increment counter
						(0 lets current ram be read)
K	1 (value)			1 (error)		write rambyte
								(counter incremented after)
L	1 (0)				1 (0)			go idle
```

### Listing Files on Camera with gphoto2

gphoto2 --list-files

### libgphoto2: Capture Command

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/konica/qm150.txt

The capture command writes a 3-byte sequence (1B 52 <nr>) to initiate image capture. The parameter '<nr>' can be either '1' or '0'. The command expects a 1-byte NACK/ACK response.

```c
1B 52 <nr>                       ESC R x
```

### Command and Response Codes

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/barbie/Protocol.txt

Details of each command, its data bytes, expected response, and a description of its function.

```APIDOC
## Command and Response Codes

Cameras send response packets after sending ACK. NAKs receive no response.

| CMD | CMD DATA BYTES             | RESP DATA BYTES             | Description                                                                                                     |
|-----|----------------------------|-----------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| A   | 1 (index #)                | 1 (0)                       | Move to image index #.                                                                                          |
| B   | 2 (duration, num times)    | 1 (0)                       | Beep (duration*50ms).                                                                                           |
| E   | 1 (test char)              | 1 (test char)               | Echo (test or wake up camera).                                                                                  |
| G   | 1 (delay & retry flags)    | 1 (0, use grab image result)| Grab image - increments counter, lower nibble = self timer delay, upper nibble = retry numbers (0,16,32,64(force),112). |
| I   | 1 (0)                      | 1 (image index)             | Get image counter (use reset first to get # pics).                                                              |
| J   | 2 (value: LSB, MSB)        | 2 (error, value)            | Increment counter (0 lets current RAM be read).                                                                  |
| K   | 1 (value)                  | 1 (error)                   | Write RAM byte (counter incremented after).                                                                     |
| L   | 1 (0)                      | 1 (0)                       | Go idle.                                                                                                        |
| M   | 1 (0)                      | hdr+pixel data+info         | Upload thumbnail (increments image counter & image index).                                                      |
| P   | 1 (new port value)         | 1 (old port value)          | Set port value.                                                                                                 |
| Q   | 1 (video mode)             | 1 (0)                       | Video mode (requires capture card).                                                                             |
| R   | 1 (register index)         | 1 (register value)          | Read register value (error = 0xFF).                                                                             |
| T   | 2 (min, max)               | 1 (0)                       | Set exposure threshold.                                                                                         |
| U   | 1 (0)                      | hdr+pixel data+info         | Upload image.                                                                                                   |
| V   | 1 (0)                      | version string              | Get version information.                                                                                        |
| W   | 2 (register index, value)  | 1 (0 = OK, 0xFF = ERR)      | Write register value.                                                                                           |
| X   | 1 (0)                      | 2 (min, max)                | Get exposure threshold.                                                                                         |
| Y   | 1 (0)                      | 1 (grab result code)        | Get grab result code (0x00 = successful, 0x80 = memory full, 0x81 = failed exposure).                           |
| Z   | 1 (0)                      | 1 (0)                       | Quit self test.                                                                                                 |
```

--------------------------------

### Configure Image Size with Gphoto2

### Get Device Information

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/sony-nex-5n.txt

Retrieves general information about the connected camera, including manufacturer, model, and serial number.

```APIDOC
## GET /api/device/info

### Description
Retrieves general information about the connected camera.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/api/device/info

### Parameters
None

### Request Example
None

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **manufacturer** (string) - The manufacturer of the camera.
- **model** (string) - The model name of the camera.
- **device_version** (string) - The firmware version of the camera.
- **serial_number** (string) - The unique serial number of the camera.
- **vendor_extension_id** (string) - The vendor extension identifier.
- **vendor_extension_version** (number) - The vendor extension version.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "manufacturer": "Sony Corporation",
  "model": "NEX-5N",
  "device_version": "1.0",
  "serial_number": "0000000000000000nnnnnnnnnnnnnnnn",
  "vendor_extension_id": "0x11",
  "vendor_extension_version": 100
}
```
```

### Device Property Value

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/fuji-x-t10.txt

Gets the current value of a specific device property, such as battery level.

```APIDOC
## GET /device/property/{property_code}

### Description
Retrieves the current value of a specified device property.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/device/property/{property_code}

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
- **property_code** (string) - Required - The PTP code for the device property (e.g., "0x5001" for Battery Level).

### Request Example
(No request body for GET requests)

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **property_code** (string) - The PTP code of the property.
- **value** (any) - The current value of the property. The type depends on the property.
- **read_only** (boolean) - Indicates if the property is read-only.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "property_code": "0x5001",
  "value": 3,
  "read_only": true
}
```
```

### Camera Initialization - Resume Communication Sequence

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/canon/ps350/ps350proto.txt

This sequence outlines how to resume communication at a chosen speed after initial negotiation. It mirrors the speed negotiation steps but uses a specific speed change command ('42 04') followed by a 'ping' to re-establish the connection.

```Assembly
--- Sequence ---
1. Computer sends serial break signal.
2. Camera answers with serial break.
3. Speed = 9600
4. Computer sends '42 04' (speed change).
5. Speed = 115200
6. Computer sends '00 53'.
7. Computer sends 'ping' packet.
8. Camera returns 'ping' reply.
9. Camera sends EOT packet with count=06.
10. Computer sends ACK packet with count=06.
```

--------------------------------

### Get Camera Status

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/sony-nex-5n.txt

Retrieves the current status of the camera, including battery level and PTP properties.

```APIDOC
## GET /api/camera/status

### Description
Retrieves the current status of the camera, including battery level and PTP properties.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/api/camera/status

### Parameters
None

### Request Example
None

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **battery_level** (string) - The current battery level of the camera (e.g., "100%").
- **ptp_property_d402** (string) - The value of PTP Property 0xd402.
- **ptp_property_d406** (string) - The value of PTP Property 0xd406.
- **ptp_property_d407** (string) - The value of PTP Property 0xd407.
- **ptp_property_d303** (string) - The value of PTP Property 0xd303.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "battery_level": "100%",
  "ptp_property_d402": "NEX-5N",
  "ptp_property_d406": "",
  "ptp_property_d407": "1",
  "ptp_property_d303": "1"
}
```
```

### Get Device Info

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/nikon-aw110.txt

Retrieves detailed information about the connected camera device, including manufacturer, model, and firmware version.

```APIDOC
## GET /gphoto/libgphoto2/deviceinfo

### Description
Retrieves detailed information about the connected camera device.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/gphoto/libgphoto2/deviceinfo

### Parameters
None

### Request Example
```json
{}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **manufacturer** (string) - Camera Manufacturer.
- **model** (string) - Camera Model.
- **device_version** (string) - Device Version.
- **serial_number** (string) - Camera Serial Number.
- **vendor_extension_id** (string) - Vendor Extension ID.
- **vendor_extension_version** (string) - Vendor Extension Version.
- **vendor_extension_description** (string) - Vendor Extension Description.
- **functional_mode** (string) - Functional Mode.
- **ptp_standard_version** (string) - PTP Standard Version.
- **supported_operations** (array) - List of supported PTP operations.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "manufacturer": "Nikon Corporation",
  "model": "AW110",
  "device_version": "COOLPIX AW110V1.1",
  "serial_number": "0000nnnnnnnn",
  "vendor_extension_id": "0x0000000a",
  "vendor_extension_version": "100",
  "vendor_extension_description": "1.0;",
  "functional_mode": "0x0000",
  "ptp_standard_version": "100",
  "supported_operations": [
    "0x1001 (get device info)",
    "0x1002 (Open session)",
    "0x1003 (Close session)",
    "0x1004 (Get storage IDs)",
    "0x1005 (Get storage info)",
    "0x1006 (Get number of objects)",
    "0x1007 (Get object handles)",
    "0x1008 (Get object info)",
    "0x1009 (Get object)",
    "0x100a (Get thumbnail)",
    "0x100b (Delete object)",
    "0x100c (Send object info)"
  ]
}
```
```

### Device Property List

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/sony-rx1rm2.txt

Retrieves a list of all configurable device properties, including their names, IDs, access types, and current values.

```APIDOC
## GET /camera/properties

### Description
Retrieves a list of all configurable device properties on the camera.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/camera/properties

### Parameters
None

### Request Example
None

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **properties** (array) - An array of objects, where each object represents a device property.
  - **id** (string) - The unique identifier for the property (e.g., "0x5004").
  - **name** (string) - The human-readable name of the property (e.g., "Compression Setting").
  - **access** (string) - Indicates if the property is readable ('read') or readable/writable ('readwrite').
  - **type** (string) - The data type of the property (e.g., "0x2" for enumeration, "0x4" for enumeration, "0x3" for enumeration, "0x6" for range).
  - **options** (object) - Contains details about the property's possible values or range.
    - **enumeration** (array) - List of possible enumerated values for the property.
    - **range** (object) - Defines the minimum, maximum, and step for a range property.
    - **step** (number) - The step increment for range properties.
    - **min** (number) - The minimum value for range properties.
    - **max** (number) - The maximum value for range properties.
  - **current_value** (any) - The current value of the property.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "properties": [
    {
      "id": "0x5004",
      "name": "Compression Setting",
      "access": "readwrite",
      "type": "0x2",
      "options": {
        "enumeration": [2, 3, 4, 16, 19]
      },
      "current_value": 3
    },
    {
      "id": "0x5005",
      "name": "White Balance",
      "access": "readwrite",
      "type": "0x4",
      "options": {
        "enumeration": [1, 2, 4, 32785, 32784, 6, 32769, 32770, 32771, 32772, 7, 32786, 32800, 32801, 32802]
      },
      "current_value": "Automatic (2)"
    },
    {
      "id": "0xd20d",
      "name": "Shutter speed",
      "access": "readwrite",
      "type": "0x6",
      "options": {
        "range": {
          "min": 0,
          "max": 4294967295,
          "step": 1
        }
      },
      "current_value": 65696
    }
  ]
}
```
```

--------------------------------

### Camera API Functions

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/doc/camlib_devel.txt

This section details the functions available in the gPhoto2 Camera API (CAPI) for interacting with camera devices.

```APIDOC
## Camera API Functions

The gPhoto2 Camera API (CAPI) provides a set of functions for controlling camera hardware and managing files.

### camera_id

#### Description
Retrieve the unique ID for the camera library.

#### Method
Function Call

#### Arguments
- **id** (CameraText *) - Unique string to represent the camera library.

#### Purpose
Ensures that only one instance of the camera library is loaded for each instance of the core. The library must copy a unique string into the `id` field.

#### Example
```c
int camera_id(CameraText *id) {
  strcpy(id->text, "my-unique-string");
  return (GP_OK);
}
```

### camera_abilities

#### Description
Retrieve the list of supported cameras and their associated abilities.

#### Method
Function Call

#### Arguments
- **list** (CameraAbilitiesList *) - The list of abilities for supported cameras.
- **count** (int *) - The number of supported cameras.

#### Purpose
Provides information about which camera models are supported and their specific capabilities (e.g., connection types, thumbnail support, file deletion).

### camera_init

#### Description
Initialize the camera device.

#### Method
Function Call

#### Arguments
- **camera** (Camera *) - Pointer to the Camera structure.
- **init** (CameraInit *) - Initialization parameters.

### camera_exit

#### Description
Close the connection to the camera device.

#### Method
Function Call

#### Arguments
- **camera** (Camera *) - Pointer to the Camera structure.

### camera_folder_list

#### Description
List the subfolders within a specified folder on the camera.

#### Method
Function Call

#### Arguments
- **camera** (Camera *) - Pointer to the Camera structure.
- **list** (CameraList *) - Structure to hold the list of subfolders.
- **folder** (char *) - The path of the folder to list contents from.

### camera_file_list

#### Description
List the files within a specified folder on the camera.

#### Method
Function Call

#### Arguments
- **camera** (Camera *) - Pointer to the Camera structure.
- **list** (CameraList *) - Structure to hold the list of files.
- **folder** (char *) - The path of the folder to list contents from.

### camera_file_get

#### Description
Retrieve a file from the camera.

#### Method
Function Call

#### Arguments
- **camera** (Camera *) - Pointer to the Camera structure.
- **folder** (char *) - The folder containing the file.
- **filename** (char *) - The name of the file to retrieve.
- **file** (CameraFile *) - Structure to hold the retrieved file data.

### camera_file_get_preview

#### Description
Retrieve a thumbnail preview of a file from the camera.

#### Method
Function Call

#### Arguments
- **camera** (Camera *) - Pointer to the Camera structure.
- **folder** (char *) - The folder containing the file.
- **filename** (char *) - The name of the file for which to get the preview.
- **file** (CameraFile *) - Structure to hold the retrieved preview data.

### camera_file_put

#### Description
Upload a file to the camera.

#### Method
Function Call

#### Arguments
- **camera** (Camera *) - Pointer to the Camera structure.
- **folder** (char *) - The destination folder on the camera.
- **filename** (char *) - The name to give the file on the camera.
- **file** (CameraFile *) - Structure containing the file data to upload.

### camera_file_delete

#### Description
Delete a file from the camera.

#### Method
Function Call

#### Arguments
- **camera** (Camera *) - Pointer to the Camera structure.
- **folder** (char *) - The folder containing the file.
- **filename** (char *) - The name of the file to delete.

### camera_config_get

#### Description
Retrieve the configuration settings for the camera.

#### Method
Function Call

#### Arguments
- **camera** (Camera *) - Pointer to the Camera structure.
- **config** (CameraConfig **) - Pointer to a structure that will hold the camera configuration.

### camera_config_set

#### Description
Set the configuration settings for the camera.

#### Method
Function Call

#### Arguments
- **camera** (Camera *) - Pointer to the Camera structure.
- **config** (CameraConfig *) - Pointer to the structure containing the new camera configuration.

### camera_capture

#### Description
Capture an image using the camera.

#### Method
Function Call

#### Arguments
- **camera** (Camera *) - Pointer to the Camera structure.
- **capturetype** (CameraCaptureType) - Type of capture to perform.

### camera_summary

#### Description
Retrieve a summary of the camera's status or capabilities.

#### Method
Function Call

#### Arguments
- **camera** (Camera *) - Pointer to the Camera structure.
- **summary** (CameraText *) - Structure to hold the camera summary string.

### camera_manual

#### Description
Perform a manual operation on the camera (e.g., manual focus adjustment).

#### Method
Function Call

#### Arguments
- **camera** (Camera *) - Pointer to the Camera structure.
- **manual** (CameraManual *) - Structure containing manual operation details.

### camera_about

#### Description
Retrieve information about the camera, such as model name and manufacturer.

#### Method
Function Call

#### Arguments
- **camera** (Camera *) - Pointer to the Camera structure.
- **about** (CameraText *) - Structure to hold the camera information string.

### Error Handling

All CAPI functions return either `GP_OK` for successful execution or `GP_ERROR` for a failure.
```

--------------------------------

### libgphoto2 PTP Property Data Example

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/nokia-808-pureview.txt

This snippet demonstrates the raw data structure for PTP (Picture Transfer Protocol) properties within libgphoto2. It represents various camera settings and their current values, including synchronization, device names, and numerical properties. The data is encoded in a way that requires parsing to be human-readable.

```text

### GET /gphoto2/properties

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/canon-eos760d.txt

Retrieves a list of device properties and their current values, including read-only and read-write properties.

```APIDOC
## GET /gphoto2/properties

### Description
Retrieves a list of device properties and their current values, including read-only and read-write properties.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/gphoto2/properties

### Parameters

None

### Request Example

None

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **properties** (array of objects) - A list of device properties.
  - **id** (string) - The property identifier (e.g., "0xd049").
  - **label** (string) - A human-readable label for the property (e.g., "Model ID").
  - **access** (string) - The access mode for the property (e.g., "read only", "readwrite").
  - **type** (string) - The data type of the property (e.g., "0x6", "0xffff", "0x2").
  - **value** (any) - The current value of the property.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "properties": [
    {
      "id": "0xd049",
      "label": "Model ID",
      "access": "read only",
      "type": "0x6",
      "value": 2147484487
    },
    {
      "id": "0xd402",
      "label": "Property 0xd402",
      "access": "read only",
      "type": "0xffff",
      "value": "Canon EOS 760D"
    },
    {
      "id": "0x5001",
      "label": "Battery Level",
      "access": "read only",
      "type": "0x2",
      "value": {
        "enumeration": [100, 0, 75, 0, 50],
        "current_percentage": 100,
        "current_value": 100
      }
    }
  ]
}
```
```

### Method

### Endpoint
/main/other/d215

### Parameters
None

  "current": 0
}
```

## PUT /main/other/d215

### Description
Sets the number of objects in memory. The value must be within the specified range.

### Method
PUT

### Endpoint
/main/other/d215

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **value** (integer) - Required - The desired number of objects in memory (0-65535).

### Request Example

}
```

### Response

- **message** (string) - Indicates success or failure of the operation.

#### Response Example

  "message": "Objects in memory set successfully"
}
```
```

### Specific Device Property API

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/canon-g9.txt

Allows getting or setting a specific device property using its ID.

```APIDOC
## GET/PUT /gphoto/libgphoto2/properties/{propertyId}

### Description
Retrieves the current value of a specific device property or updates its value. The `propertyId` is the unique identifier for the property (e.g., "0xd045").

### Method
GET (to retrieve)
PUT (to set)

### Endpoint
/gphoto/libgphoto2/properties/{propertyId}

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
- **propertyId** (string) - Required - The unique identifier of the device property (e.g., "0xd045").

#### Request Body (for PUT requests)
- **value** (any) - Required - The new value to set for the property.

### Request Example
#### GET Request:
(No request body)
`GET /gphoto/libgphoto2/properties/0xd045`

#### PUT Request:
```json
{
  "value": 5
}
```
`PUT /gphoto/libgphoto2/properties/0xd045`

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **value** (any) - The current or updated value of the property.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "value": 5
}
```
```

Fetches the number of pictures currently stored in the QV-10.

```APIDOC
## GET /camera/picture_count

### Description
Retrieves the total number of pictures stored on the QV-10 camera.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/camera/picture_count`

### Parameters
N/A

### Request Example
```hex
0x05 'MP' 0x06
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **status** (string) - Indicates successful retrieval.
- **checksum** (hex) - Checksum value (e.g., `62`).
- **picture_count** (integer) - The number of pictures in the camera.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "status": "Picture count retrieved",
  "checksum": "62",
  "picture_count": 10
}
```
```

### Example CustomFuncEx Property Value Structure

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/canon-eos-customfunc.txt

This example illustrates the detailed structure of a valid `CustomFuncEx` property value for Canon EOS cameras. It breaks down the hexadecimal-encoded numbers representing data set size, group information, function IDs, sub-values, and default states, crucial for understanding how to manipulate these settings.

```text
60,1,1,54,6, 101,1,1, 102,1,0, 104,1,0, 105,1,0, 106,2,2,1, 108,1,0

### Storage Devices API

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/canon-eos-r50.txt

Provides a summary of storage devices connected to the camera, including their description, type, capacity, and free space.

```APIDOC
## GET /storage/summary

### Description
Retrieves a summary of all storage devices detected in the camera.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/storage/summary

### Parameters
None

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **storage_devices** (object) - An object where keys are storage IDs and values contain storage details.
  - **storage_id** (string) - Identifier for the storage device.
  - **storage_description** (string) - Description of the storage media (e.g., "SD1").
  - **volume_label** (string) - The label of the storage volume.
  - **storage_type** (string) - The type of storage (e.g., "Removable RAM (memory card)").
  - **filesystem_type** (string) - The filesystem type (e.g., "Digital Camera Layout (DCIM)").
  - **access_capability** (string) - Read/write capability of the storage.
  - **maximum_capability** (string) - Total capacity of the storage in bytes and MB.
  - **free_space_bytes** (string) - Free space on the storage in bytes and MB.
  - **free_space_images** (string) - Number of images that can be stored (if available).

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "storage_devices": {
    "store_00020001": {
      "storage_description": "SD1",
      "volume_label": "",
      "storage_type": "Removable RAM (memory card)",
      "filesystem_type": "Digital Camera Layout (DCIM)",
      "access_capability": "Read-Write",
      "maximum_capability": "63831015424 (60874 MB)",
      "free_space_bytes": "54918119424 (52374 MB)",
      "free_space_images": "-1"
    }
  }
}
```
```

### Camera Settings API

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/sony-rx100m7.txt

This section covers various camera settings, including capture target, image size, ISO sensitivity, color temperature, white balance, and flash mode.

```APIDOC
## Camera Settings

### Description
This documentation details the various configurable settings for the camera, including capture destinations, image parameters, and shooting modes.

### Settings

- **/main/settings/capturetarget**
  - Label: Capture Target
  - Readonly: 0 (Writable)
  - Type: RADIO
  - Current Value: sdram
  - Choices:
    - 0: sdram
    - 1: card+sdram
    - 2: card

- **/main/imgsettings/imagesize**
  - Label: Image Size
  - Readonly: 0 (Writable)
  - Type: RADIO
  - Current Value: Large
  - Choices:
    - 0: Large
    - 1: Medium
    - 2: Small

- **/main/imgsettings/iso**
  - Label: ISO Speed
  - Readonly: 0 (Writable)
  - Type: RADIO
  - Current Value: Auto ISO

- **/main/imgsettings/colortemperature**
  - Label: Color Temperature
  - Readonly: 0 (Writable)
  - Type: RANGE
  - Current Value: 5500
  - Bottom: 2500
  - Top: 9900
  - Step: 100

- **/main/imgsettings/whitebalance**
  - Label: WhiteBalance
  - Readonly: 0 (Writable)
  - Type: RADIO
  - Current Value: Automatic
  - Choices:
    - 0: Automatic
    - 1: Daylight
    - 2: Shade
    - 3: Cloudy
    - 4: Tungsten
    - 5: Fluorescent: Warm White
    - 6: Fluorescent: Cold White
    - 7: Fluorescent: Day White
    - 8: Fluorescent: Daylight
    - 9: Flash
    - 10: Underwater: Auto
    - 11: Choose Color Temperature
    - 12: Preset 1
    - 13: Preset 2
    - 14: Preset 3

- **/main/capturesettings/zoom**
  - Label: Zoom
  - Readonly: 0 (Writable)
  - Type: RANGE
  - Current Value: 4294.97
  - Bottom: 0
  - Top: 4294.97
  - Step: 1

- **/main/capturesettings/exposurecompensation**
  - Label: Exposure Compensation
  - Readonly: 0 (Writable)
  - Type: RADIO
  - Current Value: 0

- **/main/capturesettings/flashmode**
  - Label: Flash Mode
  - Readonly: 0 (Writable)
  - Type: RADIO
  - Current Value: Fill flash
  - Choices:
    - 0: Automatic Flash
    - 1: Flash off
```

### Configure Bracketing and Lighting Optimization - libgphoto2

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/canon-powershot-sx70hs.txt

This example covers advanced shooting features like auto exposure bracketing (AEB) and auto lighting optimization. AEB captures multiple exposures for HDR, while lighting optimization adjusts contrast and brightness.

```text
/main/capturesettings/bracketmode
Label: Bracket Mode
Readonly: 0
Type: RADIO
Current: Unknown value 0000
Choice: 0 Unknown value 0000
END
/main/capturesettings/aeb
Label: Auto Exposure Bracketing
Readonly: 0
Type: RADIO
Current: off
Choice: 0 off
Choice: 1 +/- 1/3
Choice: 2 +/- 2/3
Choice: 3 +/- 1
Choice: 4 +/- 1 1/3
Choice: 5 +/- 1 2/3
Choice: 6 +/- 2
END
/main/other/alomode
Label: Auto Lighting Optimization
Readonly: 0
Type: RADIO
Current: Standard (disabled in manual exposure)
Choice: 0 x3
Choice: 1 x1
Choice: 2 Standard (disabled in manual exposure)
Choice: 3 x2
END
```

### Get Device Information

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/fuji-x-s10.txt

Retrieves general information about the connected camera, including manufacturer, model, serial number, and firmware version.

```APIDOC
## GET /api/device/info

### Description
Retrieves detailed information about the connected camera.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/api/device/info

### Parameters
None

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **manufacturer** (string) - The manufacturer of the camera.
- **model** (string) - The model name of the camera.
- **device_version** (string) - The firmware version of the camera.
- **serial_number** (string) - The unique serial number of the camera.
- **vendor_extension_id** (string) - The vendor extension identifier.
- **vendor_extension_version** (string) - The vendor extension version.
- **vendor_extension_description** (string) - A description of the vendor extension.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "manufacturer": "FUJIFILM",
  "model": "X-S10",
  "device_version": "1.01",
  "serial_number": "59xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx",
  "vendor_extension_id": "0x00000006",
  "vendor_extension_version": "100",
  "vendor_extension_description": "fujifilm.co.jp: 1.0;"
}
```
```

--------------------------------

### Ping Camera (libgphoto2 Protocol)

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/konica/qm150.txt

Initiates a ping to the camera to check for responsiveness. The camera is expected to respond with a single byte indicating ACK or an error.

```protocol
0x1B 0x58 (ESC X)
```

--------------------------------

### Supported PTP Operations (Sony ILCE-6000)

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/sony-a6000.txt

This lists the PTP operations supported by the Sony ILCE-6000 camera. These operation codes represent the commands that the camera can understand and execute, such as opening/closing sessions, getting device info, and handling objects.

```text
0x1002 (Open session)
0x1003 (Close session)
0x1001 (Get device info)
0x1004 (Get storage IDs)
0x1005 (Get storage info)
0x1006 (Get number of objects)
0x1007 (Get object handles)
0x1008 (Get object info)
0x1009 (Get object)
0x100a (Get thumbnail)
0x101b (Get partial object)
0x9201 (PTP_OC_SONY_SDIOConnect)
0x9202 (PTP_OC_SONY_GetSDIOGetExtDeviceInfo)
0x9205 (PTP_OC_SONY_SetControlDeviceA)
0x9207 (PTP_OC_SONY_SetControlDeviceB)
0x9209 (PTP_OC_SONY_GetAllDevicePropData)
```

### Get Camera Summary with gphoto2

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/nikon-j3.txt

This command retrieves a comprehensive summary of the connected camera's properties, including manufacturer, model, firmware version, storage details, and supported device settings. It's useful for understanding camera capabilities and current status.

```bash
env LANG=C gphoto2 --summary
```

### GET /main/other/d02e - PTP Property 0xd02e

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/olympus-e-m5mark2.txt

Provides information on PTP Property 0xd02e, a MENU type property with no read-only restriction and a set of numerical options.

```APIDOC
## GET /main/other/d02e

### Description
Retrieves information about PTP Property 0xd02e. This property is of type MENU and is not read-only.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/main/other/d02e

### Parameters
None

### Request Example
None

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **current_value** (number) - The current setting of the PTP property.
- **choices** (array) - An array of available choices for this property, where each choice is an object with 'index' and 'value'.

#### Response Example
{
  "current_value": 50,
  "choices": [
    {"index": 0, "value": 0},
    {"index": 1, "value": 17},
    {"index": 2, "value": 18},
    ...
  ]
}
```

--------------------------------

### GET /main/other/d03a - PTP Property 0xd03a

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/olympus-e-m5mark2.txt

Retrieve information about PTP Property 0xd03a. This property is of type MENU and is not read-only.

```APIDOC
## GET /main/other/d03a

### Description
Retrieves information about PTP Property 0xd03a. This property is of type MENU and is not read-only.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/main/other/d03a

### Parameters
None

### Request Example
None

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **current_value** (number) - The current setting of the PTP property.
- **choices** (array) - An array of available choices for this property, where each choice is an object with 'index' and 'value'.

#### Response Example
{
  "current_value": 0,
  "choices": [
    {"index": 0, "value": 65529},
    {"index": 1, "value": 65530},
    {"index": 2, "value": 65531},
    ...
  ]
}
```

### Settings Management

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/canon-powershot-g7x.txt

Manage camera settings such as date and time, owner name, and capture target.

```APIDOC
## PUT /gphoto2/camera/settings/datetime

### Description
Sets the camera's date and time.

### Method
PUT

### Endpoint
/gphoto2/camera/settings/datetime

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **timestamp** (integer) - Required - The new timestamp (Unix epoch time) for the camera's date and time. Use 'now' to set the current time.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "timestamp": 1678886400 
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **message** (string) - Confirmation message indicating the date and time were updated.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "message": "Camera date and time updated successfully."
}
```
```

```APIDOC
## PUT /gphoto2/camera/settings/ownername

### Description
Sets the owner's name for the camera.

### Method
PUT

### Endpoint
/gphoto2/camera/settings/ownername

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **name** (string) - Required - The name of the owner.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "name": "John Doe"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **message** (string) - Confirmation message indicating the owner name was updated.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "message": "Owner name updated successfully."
}
```
```

```APIDOC
## PUT /gphoto2/camera/settings/capturetarget

### Description
Sets the target location for captured images.

### Method
PUT

### Endpoint
/gphoto2/camera/settings/capturetarget

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **target** (string) - Required - The capture target (e.g., "Internal RAM", "Memory card").

### Request Example
```json
{
  "target": "Memory card"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **message** (string) - Confirmation message indicating the capture target was updated.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "message": "Capture target updated successfully."
}
```
```

### Get Camera Settings

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/nikon-aw110.txt

Retrieves the current configuration values for various camera settings. This endpoint provides a comprehensive list of available settings and their current states.

```APIDOC
## GET /gphoto/libgphoto2/config

### Description
Retrieves the current configuration values for various camera settings.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/gphoto/libgphoto2/config

### Parameters
None

### Request Example
```json
{}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **autofocusdrive** (TOGGLE) - Drive Nikon DSLR Autofocus status.
- **controlmode** (TEXT) - Nikon Control Mode setting.
- **viewfinder** (TOGGLE) - Nikon Viewfinder status.
- **datetime** (DATE) - Camera Date and Time.
- **guid** (TEXT) - WLAN GUID.
- **fastfs** (TOGGLE) - Fast Filesystem status.
- **capturetarget** (RADIO) - Capture Target setting (Internal RAM or Memory card).
- **serialnumber** (TEXT) - Camera Serial Number.
- **manufacturer** (TEXT) - Camera Manufacturer.
- **cameramodel** (TEXT) - Camera Model.
- **deviceversion** (TEXT) - Device Version.
- **vendorextension** (TEXT) - Vendor Extension information.
- **flashmode** (RADIO) - Flash Mode setting.
- **f-number** (RADIO) - F-Number setting.
- **imagequality** (RADIO) - Image Quality setting.
- **focallength** (RANGE) - Focal Length setting.
- **focusmode** (RADIO) - Focus Mode setting.
- **expprogram** (RADIO) - Exposure Program setting.
- **shutterspeed2** (RADIO) - Shutter Speed 2 setting.
- **liveviewafmode** (RADIO) - Live View AF Mode setting.
- **battery_level** (MENU) - Battery Level.
- **compression_setting** (MENU) - Compression Setting.
- **focus_mode_menu** (MENU) - Focus Mode (Menu).
- **flash_mode_menu** (MENU) - Flash Mode (Menu).
- **exposure_program_mode** (MENU) - Exposure Program Mode (Menu).
- **date_time** (TEXT) - Date & Time.
- **ptp_property_d002** (MENU) - PTP Property 0xd002.
- **live_view_af_area** (RANGE) - Live View AF Area.
- **lens_sort** (MENU) - Lens Sort.
- **nikon_exposure_time** (MENU) - Nikon Exposure Time.
- **live_view_status** (MENU) - Live View Status.
- **live_view_prohibit_condition** (TEXT) - Live View Prohibit Condition.
- **ptp_property_d1ac** (MENU) - PTP Property 0xd1ac.
- **ptp_property_d24f** (TEXT) - PTP Property 0xd24f.
- **ptp_property_d250** (TEXT) - PTP Property 0xd250.
- **ptp_property_d251** (TEXT) - PTP Property 0xd251.
- **ptp_property_d407** (TEXT) - PTP Property 0xd407.
- **ptp_property_d303** (TEXT) - PTP Property 0xd303.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "autofocusdrive": 0,
  "controlmode": "0",

  "f-number": "f/3.9",
  "imagequality": "JPEG Normal",
  "focallength": {
    "current": 35,
    "bottom": 35,
    "top": 105,
    "step": 1
  },
  "focusmode": "AF-S",
  "expprogram": "Auto",
  "shutterspeed2": "1/60",
  "liveviewafmode": "Unknown value 0002",

    "current": 2,

### Camera Settings API

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/sony-a7r3a.txt

Configure various camera settings such as capture target and image size.

```APIDOC
## POST /main/settings/capturetarget

### Description
Sets the target for image capture (e.g., SD card, internal memory).

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/main/settings/capturetarget

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **value** (string) - Required - The desired capture target. Accepted values: "sdram", "card+sdram".

### Request Example
```json
{
  "value": "card+sdram"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **message** (string) - Confirmation of the capture target setting.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "message": "Capture target set to card+sdram."
}
```

## POST /main/imgsettings/imagesize

### Description
Sets the image size for captured photos.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/main/imgsettings/imagesize

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **value** (string) - Required - The desired image size. Accepted values: "Large", "Medium", "Small".

### Request Example
```json
{
  "value": "Medium"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **message** (string) - Confirmation of the image size setting.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "message": "Image size set to Medium."
}
```

## POST /main/imgsettings/iso

### Description
Sets the ISO speed for image capture.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/main/imgsettings/iso

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **value** (string) - Required - The desired ISO speed. Accepted values include "Auto ISO", "100", "200", etc., up to "409600". Also supports multi-frame noise reduction options.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "value": "400"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **message** (string) - Confirmation of the ISO speed setting.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "message": "ISO speed set to 400."
}
```
```

### Allocate Bandwidth for ISO Transfers (640x480) using Blink2

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/sipix/blink2.txt

Allocates bandwidth for ISO transfers, specifically for a 640x480 resolution. This command is used in conjunction with video streaming initiation.

```protocol
640x480: control read 0x15, 0x0, 0x00	-> buf[1]
```

### Reproducing Bugs with Debug Output (Shell)

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/README.md

This snippet demonstrates how to run applications with debug logging enabled and set the locale to English for consistent bug reporting. It covers both the gtkam frontend and the gphoto2 command-line interface. Ensure you have the respective tools installed.

```shell
env LC_ALL=C gtkam
```

```shell
env LC_ALL=C gphoto2 --debug-logfile=logfile.log --debug <options>
```

### libgphoto2 Command Reference (Y-Z)

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/barbie/Protocol.txt

Details the commands from 'Y' to 'Z' for the libgphoto2 protocol. Includes command data bytes, response data bytes, and a description of the command's function.

```text
CMD	CMD DATA BYTES		RESP DATA BYTES		Description
---	-----------------------	---------------------	-----------------------
Y	1 (0)				1 (grab result code)	get grab result code
						0x00 = successful
						0x80 = memory full
						0x81 = failed exposure
Z	1 (0)				1 (0)			quit self test
```

--------------------------------

### Libgphoto2 Extended Device Information and Thumbnail Commands

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/canon-powershot-sx70hs.txt

This snippet focuses on extended device information retrieval and thumbnail handling. It includes commands for getting extended object information and thumbnails, as well as specific EOS commands for managing partial object transfers.

```log
0.714364 print_debug_deviceinfo      (2):   0x9109 (EOS_GetObjectInfoEx)
0.714380 print_debug_deviceinfo      (2):   0x9173 (EOS_GetObjectInfoEx64)
0.714396 print_debug_deviceinfo      (2):   0x910a (EOS_GetThumbEx)
0.714412 print_debug_deviceinfo      (2):   0x9132 (EOS_EndGetPartialObjectEx)
```

### GET /main/other/d038 - PTP Property 0xd038

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/olympus-e-m5mark2.txt

Provides information on PTP Property 0xd038, a MENU type property that is not read-only and presents several numerical options.

```APIDOC
## GET /main/other/d038

### Description
Retrieves information about PTP Property 0xd038. This property is of type MENU and is not read-only.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/main/other/d038

### Parameters
None

### Request Example
None

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **current_value** (number) - The current setting of the PTP property.
- **choices** (array) - An array of available choices for this property, where each choice is an object with 'index' and 'value'.

#### Response Example
{
  "current_value": 0,
  "choices": [
    {"index": 0, "value": 65529},
    {"index": 1, "value": 65530},
    {"index": 2, "value": 65531},
    ...
  ]
}
```

### PTP Property 0xd217 Configuration

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/sony-rx100m7.txt

Allows setting and getting a PTP-specific property identified by 0xd217. This is a MENU type property.

```APIDOC
## GET /main/other/d217

### Description
Retrieves the current value of PTP Property 0xd217.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/main/other/d217

### Parameters
None

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **current** (integer) - The current value of the PTP property.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "current": 1
}
```

## PUT /main/other/d217

### Description
Sets the value of PTP Property 0xd217.

### Method
PUT

### Endpoint
/main/other/d217

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **value** (integer) - Required - The desired value for PTP Property 0xd217.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "value": 0
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **message** (string) - Indicates success or failure of the operation.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "message": "PTP Property 0xd217 set successfully"
}
```
```

### Get Device Property API

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/olympus-e-pm1.txt

Retrieves the value of a specific device property.

```APIDOC
## GET /api/device/property/{propertyId}

### Description
Retrieves the value of a specific device property.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/api/device/property/{propertyId}

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
- **propertyId** (string) - Required - The ID of the device property to retrieve (e.g., '5011' for Date & Time).

### Request Example
```json
{
  "propertyId": "5011"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - The ID of the property.
- **label** (string) - The human-readable label of the property.
- **readonly** (integer) - Indicates if the property is read-only (0 for writable, 1 for read-only).
- **type** (string) - The data type of the property (e.g., 'TEXT').
- **current** (string) - The current value of the property.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "id": "/main/other/5011",
  "label": "Date & Time",
  "readonly": 0,
  "type": "TEXT",
  "current": "20110101T000000"
}
```
```

### Get Device Info API

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/olympus-e-pm1.txt

Retrieves general information about the connected device, such as manufacturer, model, serial number, and supported PTP versions.

```APIDOC
## GET /api/device/info

### Description
Retrieves general information about the connected device.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/api/device/info

### Parameters
None

### Request Example
```json
{}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **manufacturer** (string) - The manufacturer of the device.
- **model** (string) - The model of the device.
- **deviceVersion** (string) - The firmware version of the device.
- **serialNumber** (string) - The serial number of the device.
- **vendorExtensionId** (string) - The vendor extension ID.
- **vendorExtensionVersion** (string) - The vendor extension version.
- **vendorExtensionDescription** (string) - The vendor extension description.
- **functionalMode** (string) - The functional mode of the device.
- **ptpStandardVersion** (string) - The PTP standard version supported by the device.
- **supportedOperations** (array) - A list of supported operations codes.
- **eventsSupported** (array) - A list of supported event codes.
- **devicePropertiesSupported** (array) - A list of supported device property codes.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "manufacturer": "OLYMPUS",
  "model": "E-PM1",
  "deviceVersion": "1.00",
  "serialNumber": "'BBnnnnnnn'",
  "vendorExtensionId": "0x00000006",
  "vendorExtensionVersion": "100",
  "vendorExtensionDescription": null,
  "functionalMode": "0x0000",
  "ptpStandardVersion": "100",
  "supportedOperations": [
    "0x1001",
    "0x1002",
    "0x1003",
    "0x1004",
    "0x1005",
    "0x1006",
    "0x1007",
    "0x1008",
    "0x1009",
    "0x100a",
    "0x100b",
    "0x100f",
    "0x1014",
    "0x1015",
    "0x1016",
    "0x101b",
    "0x9801",
    "0x9802",
    "0x9803",
    "0x9805"
  ],
  "eventsSupported": [
    "0x4004",
    "0x4005",
    "0x4002",
    "0x4009"
  ],
  "devicePropertiesSupported": [
    "0x5001",
    "0x5011",
    "0xd405",
    "0xd406",
    "0xd407"
  ]
}
```
```

## Settings Endpoints

### Description
Provides endpoints to control and view camera settings, including owner name, capture target, and time synchronization.

`/gphoto/libgphoto2` (Conceptual - endpoints represent specific settings)

### Parameters
None (Specific parameters depend on the setting being accessed)

### Example Endpoints and Actions

*   **/main/actions/syncdatetime**
    *   **Label**: Synchronize camera date and time with PC
    *   **Type**: TOGGLE
    *   **Current**: 0

*   **/main/settings/ownername**
    *   **Label**: Owner Name
    *   **Type**: TEXT
    *   **Current**: ""

*   **/main/settings/capturetarget**
    *   **Label**: Capture Target
    *   **Type**: RADIO
    *   **Current**: "Memory card"
    *   **Choices**: 
        *   0: "Internal RAM"
        *   1: "Memory card"

*   **/main/settings/capture**
    *   **Label**: Capture
    *   **Type**: TOGGLE
    *   **Current**: 0

### Response Example (Illustrative for changing owner name)

{
  "status": "success",
  "message": "Owner name updated."
}
```
```

### Camera Settings

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/nikon-z6-2.txt

Endpoints for configuring general camera settings such as date/time, image comments, recording media, and flicker reduction.

```APIDOC
## Camera Settings API

### Description
This section provides endpoints for managing various camera settings.

### Camera Date and Time
- **Endpoint**: `/main/settings/datetime`
- **Label**: Camera Date and Time
- **Method**: GET/PUT
- **Type**: DATE
- **Description**: Sets or retrieves the camera's date and time.
- **Help**: Use 'now' as the current time when setting.

### Image Comment
- **Endpoint**: `/main/settings/imagecomment`
- **Label**: Image Comment
- **Method**: GET/PUT
- **Type**: TEXT
- **Description**: Sets or retrieves the image comment.

### Enable Image Comment
- **Endpoint**: `/main/settings/imagecommentenable`
- **Label**: Enable Image Comment
- **Method**: GET/PUT
- **Type**: RADIO
- **Description**: Enables or disables the image comment feature.
- **Choices**: 0 (Off), 1 (On)

### Recording Media
- **Endpoint**: `/main/settings/recordingmedia`
- **Label**: Recording Media
- **Method**: GET/PUT
- **Type**: RADIO
- **Description**: Selects the recording media.
- **Choices**: 0 (Card), 1 (SDRAM), 2 (Unknown value 0002)

### Artist
- **Endpoint**: `/main/settings/artist`
- **Label**: Artist
- **Method**: GET/PUT
- **Type**: TEXT
- **Description**: Sets or retrieves the artist information.

### Copyright
- **Endpoint**: `/main/settings/copyright`
- **Label**: Copyright
- **Method**: GET/PUT
- **Type**: TEXT
- **Description**: Sets or retrieves the copyright information.

### Clean Sensor
- **Endpoint**: `/main/settings/cleansensor`
- **Label**: Clean Sensor
- **Method**: GET/PUT
- **Type**: RADIO
- **Description**: Initiates the sensor cleaning process.
- **Choices**: 0 (Off), 1 (Shutdown)

### Flicker Reduction
- **Endpoint**: `/main/settings/flickerreduction`
- **Label**: Flicker Reduction
- **Method**: GET/PUT
- **Type**: RADIO
- **Description**: Configures flicker reduction settings.
- **Choices**: 0 (50 Hz), 1 (60 Hz), 2 (Unknown value 00ff)

### Thumb Size
- **Endpoint**: `/main/settings/thumbsize`
- **Label**: Thumb Size
- **Method**: GET/PUT
- **Type**: RADIO
- **Description**: Sets the thumbnail size.
- **Choices**: 0 (normal), 1 (large)

### Fast Filesystem
- **Endpoint**: `/main/settings/fastfs`
- **Label**: Fast Filesystem
- **Method**: GET/PUT
- **Type**: TOGGLE
- **Description**: Enables or disables the fast filesystem.

### Capture Target
- **Endpoint**: `/main/settings/capturetarget`
- **Label**: Capture Target
- **Method**: GET/PUT
- **Type**: RADIO
- **Description**: Sets the target for image capture.
- **Choices**: 0 (Internal RAM), 1 (Memory card)

### Autofocus
- **Endpoint**: `/main/settings/autofocus`
- **Label**: Autofocus
- **Method**: GET/PUT
- **Type**: RADIO
- **Description**: Enables or disables autofocus.
- **Choices**: 0 (On), 1 (Off)

```

--------------------------------

### GET /camera/picture/{picture_number}

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/casio/PROTOCOL.txt

Displays a specific picture on the QV-10's LCD.

```APIDOC
## GET /camera/picture/{picture_number}

### Description
Displays a specified picture on the QV-10's LCD screen.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/camera/picture/{picture_number}`

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
- **picture_number** (hex) - Required - The number of the picture to display (e.g., `XX`).

### Request Example
```hex
0x05 'DA' XX 0x06
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **status** (string) - Indicates the picture is being displayed.
- **checksum** (hex) - Checksum value (e.g., `YY`).

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "status": "Picture displayed",
  "checksum": "7a"
}
```

### Notes
The checksum `YY` is calculated as `0x7a - picture_number`.
```

--------------------------------

#### Response Example
{
  "current": "Flash",
  "choices": [
    "Auto",
    "Daylight",
    "Shadow",
    "Cloudy",
    "Tungsten",
    "Fluorescent",
    "Flash",
    "Manual",
    "Color Temperature",
    "AWB White"
  ]
}
```

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/olympus-e-m5mark2.txt

Details for PTP Property 0xd02f, a configurable MENU type property offering specific numerical choices.

```APIDOC
## GET /main/other/d02f

### Description
Retrieves information about PTP Property 0xd02f. This property is of type MENU and is not read-only.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/main/other/d02f

### Parameters
None

### Request Example
None

### Response
#### Success Response (200)

- **choices** (array) - An array of available choices for this property, where each choice is an object with 'index' and 'value'.

#### Response Example
{
  "current_value": 34,
  "choices": [
    {"index": 0, "value": 0},
    {"index": 1, "value": 17},
    {"index": 2, "value": 18},
    ...
  ]
}
```

### List All Camera Configurations using gphoto2

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/canon-eos90d.txt

This command lists all configurable settings for the connected camera, including their labels, read-only status, types, current values, and available choices for RADIO and TOGGLE types. It's essential for understanding and manipulating camera parameters via the command line. Dependencies include the gphoto2 utility and a connected camera.

```bash
LANG=C gphoto2 --list-all-config
```

### Open Session PTP Command in Python

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/canon-eos-discovery.md

This example demonstrates how to open a PTP session using the miniPtp transaction function. It uses the code 0x1002 and provides the session ID as a request parameter, with no data phase involved.

```python
self.transaction( 0x1002, [ self.session_id ], False )
```

### Retrieve File (RETR)

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ricoh/g3.txt

Downloads a file from the camera. Initiates a data connection and transfers the file data, followed by a success message.

```text
RETR file"		- 150 data connection for RETR.(%d)
			  ... data , %d bytes ...
			  250 RETR command success.
```

--------------------------------

### Get Camera Status 2 (libgphoto2)

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/sigma-fp.txt

Retrieves extended camera status information. This command (0x902c) takes three arguments, typically all zeros, and returns a fixed amount of data (0x44 bytes). The response includes directory structure information with tags, data types, counts, and offsets.

```c
/* Opcode: 0x902c */
/* Arguments: 0x0, 0x0, 0x0 */
/* Response size: 0x44 bytes */
/* Response structure:
   dword length
   dword nrofdirs
   dir[]:
     word tagtype
     word datatype
     dword count
     dword valueoffset
*/

// Example response snippet:
// 0x902c recv data from cam: 0x44 bytes
// ... (data payload follows)
```

### File Operations

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/doc/camlib_devel.txt

Functions for retrieving, uploading, and deleting files from a camera.

```APIDOC
## GET /gphoto2/camera/file

### Description
Retrieves a file from the camera.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/gphoto2/camera/file

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters

- **filename** (string) - Required - The name of the file to retrieve.

### Response

- **file_content** (binary) - The content of the retrieved file.

## POST /gphoto2/camera/file

### Description
Uploads a file to the camera.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/gphoto2/camera/file

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **folder** (string) - Required - The destination folder path on the camera.

#### Request Body
- **file** (binary) - Required - The file to upload.

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **message** (string) - Confirmation of successful upload.

## DELETE /gphoto2/camera/file

### Description
Deletes a file from the camera.

### Method
DELETE

### Endpoint
/gphoto2/camera/file

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **folder** (string) - Required - The folder path of the file on the camera.
- **filename** (string) - Required - The name of the file to delete.

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **message** (string) - Confirmation of successful deletion.
```

This snippet illustrates the logging of camera property descriptions, indicated by 'event XXX: EOS prop YYY desc record'. It includes details like datasize, propxtype, and property identifiers.

```log
event 189: EOS prop d10b desc record, datasize 0, propxtype 3
event 190: EOS prop d10c desc record, datasize 0, propxtype 3
event 191: EOS prop d10d desc record, datasize 0, propxtype 3
```

### Display Supported Operations with gphoto2

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/sony-hx90v.txt

Lists all supported PTP operations for the connected camera. This information helps in understanding the capabilities of the camera's PTP interface and which commands can be sent to it. It's useful for developing custom camera control applications.

```bash
# Supported operations:
  0x1002 (Open session)
  0x1003 (Close session)
  0x1001 (Get device info)
  0x1004 (Get storage IDs)
  0x1005 (Get storage info)
  0x1006 (Get number of objects)
  0x1007 (Get object handles)
  0x1008 (Get object info)
  0x1009 (Get object)
  0x100a (Get thumbnail)
  0x1014 (Get device property description)
  0x1015 (Get device property value)
  0x1016 (Set device property value)
  0x101b (Get partial object)
  0x9801 (Unknown PTP_OC)
  0x9802 (Unknown PTP_OC)
  0x9803 (Unknown PTP_OC)
  0x9805 (Unknown PTP_OC)
  0x9280 (Unknown PTP_OC)
  0x9281 (Unknown PTP_OC)
  0x9282 (Unknown PTP_OC)
  0x9283 (Unknown PTP_OC)
  0x9284 (Unknown PTP_OC)
  0x9285 (Unknown PTP_OC)
```

### GET /camera/picture/data/{picture_number}

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/casio/PROTOCOL.txt

Retrieves picture data in JPEG format from the QV-10.

```APIDOC
## GET /camera/picture/data/{picture_number}

### Description
Fetches picture data from the QV-10 in JPEG format.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/camera/picture/data/{picture_number}`

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
- **picture_number** (hex) - Required - The number of the picture to retrieve (e.g., `XX`).

### Request Example
```hex
0x05 'DA' XX 0x06 0x05 'DL' 0x06 0x05 'MG' 0x06 0x12
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **status** (string) - Indicates successful data retrieval.
- **checksum_xx** (hex) - Checksum for the picture number (e.g., `YY`, where `YY = 0x7a - XX`).
- **checksum_6f** (hex) - Checksum `6f`.
- **checksum_6b** (hex) - Checksum `6b`.
- **picture_data** (bytes) - The actual JPEG picture data.
- **end_marker** (hex) - The end marker `02 00 00 03 FC`.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "status": "Picture data retrieved",
  "checksum_xx": "7a",
  "checksum_6f": "6f",
  "checksum_6b": "6b",
  "picture_data": "...[binary data]...",
  "end_marker": "02000003FC"
}
```

### Notes
- For QV100 'fine mode' pictures, use 'Mg' instead of 'MG'.
- The `picture_data` format includes a block size (2 bytes), image data, and a checksum.
```

--------------------------------

- **type** (string) - The type of setting (e.g., 'MENU').
- **current** (string) - The current DRangeOptimize value.
- **choices** (array) - An array of available DRangeOptimize choices.
  - **id** (string) - The identifier for the choice.
  - **label** (string) - The human-readable label for the choice.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "label": "DRangeOptimize",
  "readonly": 0,

### Focus Mode Configuration

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/sony-rx100m7.txt

Allows setting and getting the camera's focus mode. This is a MENU type property with predefined choices.

```APIDOC
## GET /main/other/500a

### Description
Retrieves the current focus mode of the camera.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/main/other/500a

### Parameters
None

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **current** (integer) - The current focus mode. See choices for possible values.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "current": 1
}
```

## PUT /main/other/500a

### Description
Sets the focus mode of the camera. Use one of the available choice values.

### Method
PUT

### Endpoint
/main/other/500a

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **value** (integer) - Required - The desired focus mode. Possible values include: 0 (2), 1 (32773), 2 (32772), 3 (32774), 4 (1).

### Request Example
```json
{
  "value": 0
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **message** (string) - Indicates success or failure of the operation.

#### Response Example
```json
{

--------------------------------

### Get Picture Information Command

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/casio/PROTOCOL.txt

Details the command sequence for retrieving specific picture information. It includes commands for data acquisition ('DA', 'DL') and camera settings retrieval ('CV'). Checksum calculations and data field interpretations are provided.

```protocol
GET PICTURE INFORMATION
=======================
    05 'DA' XX 06 05  'DL' 06
    -------------------------
     06      YY     06   6f  

    05  'CV'  06  12                             06
    -------------------------------------------------------------
      06   66       02 00 0b [11bytes data] 17 SS  02 00 00 03 FC

Comment:
    XX is the picture number.
    The return byte YY is checksum. (0x7a - XX).
    Return byte 6f is checksum.
    Return byte 66 is checksum.
    SS: Check sum.  Reverse bits of all sum of second byte (after 0x02) 
        of data block to before SS (0x17).

    11bytes data
     1st byte Compression  01:economy 02:normal 03:fine
     2nd byte unknown 00
     3rd byte taked mode   01:one shot 02:continuous shot
                           07:panorama 08:movie
     4th byte macro mode   01:normal 02:macro mode
     5th byte unknown 01
     6th byte unknown 0a,09,0c,0e,0b shutter speed? WB?
     7th byte iris(maybe) 07:(F8) 03:(F2)
     8th byte unknown 0d
     9th byte unknown 04
    10th byte unknown 0d
    11th byte unknown 01
```

--------------------------------

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/agfa-cl20/protocol2.txt

This SetupPacket is used to initiate the transfer of Exif files. Similar to image information requests, there are variations for 'flash card' and 'non flash card' modes, suggesting different protocols or data handling for each scenario.

```text
flash card: 41 0a 01 00 0a 00 00 00
non flash card: 41 03 ff 0f 08 00 00 00

### Download Table of Contents (File Directory)

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/enigma13/protocol.txt

This snippet details the process of downloading the camera's file directory (Table of Contents). It involves sending a USB_WRITE command to request the TOC, followed by setup packet reads. The directory entries contain the image name (16 bytes) and size (16 bytes). The size is represented in a specific byte format that needs parsing.

```plaintext
USB_WRITE COMMAND TO REQUEST THE TOC:
41 54 08 00 01 00 00 00

<- 41
-> c1 21 00 00 00 00 01 00     (SETUP PACKET READ. don't know what for)

<- 01
->c1 21 00 00 02 00 01 00a     (SETUP PACKET READ. don't know what for)

Then you can read (32* number_of_images)

Example TOC entry data:
00000000: 53 55 4e 50 30 30 30 31 4a 50 47 20 00 00 00 00
00000010: 00 00 c3 0b 00 00 7d 1a c3 0b 04 00 8e 75 03 00

Toc entry description:
This is the 1st picture :
the name is SUNP0001JPG ( 53 55 4e 50 30 30 30 31 4a 50 47 20 ) in ASCII
the size is 0x03<<10000 +  0x75<<100 +  08e  =0x03758e  == 226702 bytes
```

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/nikon-d3200.txt

The `gphoto2 --list-all-config` command enumerates all configurable settings for the connected camera, including their labels, types, current values, and available choices for radio or enumeration types. This is essential for scripting camera adjustments. Dependencies include the `gphoto2` utility and a connected camera.

Current: nnnnnnn0000000000000000000000000
/main/status/manufacturer

Type: TEXT
Current: Nikon Corporation
/main/status/cameramodel

/main/status/deviceversion

/main/status/vendorextension
Label: Vendor Extension
Type: TEXT
Current: microsoft.com: 1.0
/main/status/batterylevel
Label: Battery Level
Type: TEXT
Current: 35%
/main/imgsettings/imagesize
Label: Image Size
Type: RADIO
Current: 6016x4000
Choice: 0 6016x4000
Choice: 1 4512x3000
Choice: 2 3008x2000

### Get Firmware ID using Blink2 Protocol

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/sipix/blink2.txt

Retrieves the firmware identification from the camera using a Blink2 control read command. It expects a 6-byte buffer as output.

```protocol
control read 0x18, 0x03, 0x00	-> buf[6]
```

/main/other/d214

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **value** (integer) - Required - The desired value for PTP Property 0xd214 (0 to 4.29497e+09).

### Request Example
```json
{
  "value": 1000000000
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **message** (string) - Indicates success or failure of the operation.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "message": "PTP Property 0xd214 set successfully"
}
```
```

--------------------------------

### Show Test Color Pattern (libgphoto2)

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/casio/PROTOCOL.txt

Displays a test color pattern on the camera's LCD. The command is 'DP', followed by a checksum byte.

```text
05  'DP' 06
-------------
  06   XX 

Comment:
    Show 'test color patten' on LCD.
    The return byte XX is checksum.
```

--------------------------------

### Get Size of Input Data to Camera

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/canon-powershot-sx160is.txt

Retrieves the size of input data that can be sent to the camera.

```APIDOC
## GET /gphoto/libgphoto2/main/other/d02f

### Description
Retrieves the size of data that can be sent as input to the camera.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/gphoto/libgphoto2/main/other/d02f

### Parameters
This endpoint does not accept any parameters.

### Request Body
This endpoint does not accept a request body.

### Request Example
```json
{}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **size_input_data** (integer) - The size of input data in bytes.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "size_input_data": 524288
}
```
```

### GET /main/capturesettings/meteringmode

```APIDOC
## GET /main/capturesettings/meteringmode

### Description
Gets the current metering mode, which determines how the camera measures light to calculate exposure.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/main/capturesettings/meteringmode

### Parameters
None

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **current** (string) - The current metering mode (e.g., "Spot", "Evaluative", "Center-weighted average").

  "current": "Evaluative"
}
```
```

### Store File (-STOR)

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ricoh/g3.txt

Uploads a file to the camera. Requires specifying the file size. The command involves a data transfer phase and a success confirmation.

```text
-STOR size filename"	- 150 ... 
			  ... data transfer ... 
			  200 done
```

```APIDOC
## GET /main/capturesettings/shutterspeed

Gets the current shutter speed setting of the camera. Shutter speed controls the duration the camera's sensor is exposed to light, affecting motion blur.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/main/capturesettings/shutterspeed

### Parameters
None

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **current** (string) - The current shutter speed setting (e.g., "1/80", "30").

#### Response Example

  "current": "1/80"
}
```
```

### Get Device Version

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/nikon-d4.txt

This action retrieves the version information for the camera's firmware or device. The type is TEXT.

```text
/main/status/deviceversion
Label: Device Version
Type: TEXT
Current: V1.02
```

--------------------------------

### GET /main/other/d030 - PTP Property 0xd030

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/camlibs/ptp2/cameras/olympus-e-m5mark2.txt

Information on PTP Property 0xd030, a mutable MENU type property presenting a defined range of numerical options.

```APIDOC
## GET /main/other/d030

### Description
Retrieves information about PTP Property 0xd030. This property is of type MENU and is not read-only.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/main/other/d030

### Parameters
None

### Request Example
None

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **current_value** (number) - The current setting of the PTP property.
- **choices** (array) - An array of available choices for this property, where each choice is an object with 'index' and 'value'.

#### Response Example
{
  "current_value": 18,
  "choices": [
    {"index": 0, "value": 0},
    {"index": 1, "value": 17},
    {"index": 2, "value": 18},
    ...
  ]
}
```

### Camera File Data and Conversion

Source: https://github.com/gphoto/libgphoto2/blob/master/doc/api/gphoto2-sections.txt

Functions for getting and setting file data, as well as converting file formats. Supports various image and audio types.

```C
gp_file_get_data_and_size(file, data, size)
gp_file_set_data_and_size(file, data, size)
gp_file_convert(file, mime_type)
```
